# Production readiness: the MC compiler (`mcc`)

Status: **qualified subset, not generally production-ready**.
Current assessment: **updated 2026-07-10, based on the current compiler worktree**.
Evidence register: **438 bounded implementation or regression entries, 1 active slice, 3 open architectural workstreams**.

The compiler has locally verified behavior across its supported subset. It is not
ready for an unrestricted production claim because pointer-provenance race
lowering, typed-MIR ownership of semantic facts, and CFG/place-based move analysis
still have open architectural closure boundaries.

The evidence count is an audit register, not a completion percentage. The three
closure matrices below, rather than the evidence count, define the exit criteria
for a general production-ready claim.

## 0. Current Assessment

### Current Guarantee

Within the tested supported subset, the compiler either emits the documented
lowering or rejects unsupported cases explicitly. Unknown scalar pointer
dereferences use conservative race-tolerant lowering where supported.

This document does not claim complete correctness for arbitrary pointer-return
flow, arbitrary aggregate-return CFG, or general CFG-based move ownership.

### Evidence Model

- A **finished** row means one bounded behavior or regression-evidence slice is
  locally verified and tied to concrete evidence. Evidence-only rows must say so;
  they do not advance an umbrella's closure matrix by themselves.
- An **active** row means one bounded behavior is actively being changed and
  still needs evidence before it can move to finished. It is not counted as
  completed evidence and must not change the supported-subset claim.
- An **open architectural workstream** is larger than one implementation slice. Its
  count should not drop just because another narrow case lands; it drops only
  when the workstream's acceptance boundary is either fully closed or explicitly
  narrowed by project decision.
- Historical sections after the evidence register are audit context. When they
  conflict with this assessment, this assessment is the current source of truth.
- The open-workstream count is not a percentage. The workstreams overlap but
  are not interchangeable; progress is reported by closure-matrix rows, not by
  adding completed evidence entries.

### Evidence Register

| Item | Why it matters | Evidence |
|---|---|---|
| Parser nesting is bounded | Deep input now produces a diagnostic instead of a compiler crash. | `E_NESTING_TOO_DEEP`; direct deep-paren probe rejects cleanly. |
| Parser recovery reports multiple parse errors across scoped bodies | Top-level declarations, block statements, module/impl/trait members, and aggregate fields now resync inside the enclosing syntax body; parse-failed modules still abort before sema, avoiding misleading semantic follow-on errors. | `7d705b12 Improve parser declaration recovery`; `tests/spec/parser_statement_recovery.mc`; `tests/spec/parser_declaration_recovery.mc`; direct `mcc check` emits multiple parse diagnostics without orphan-brace noise. |
| Missing imports and cross-file diagnostics are actionable | Users see the failing import path or imported file/line instead of root-file noise or raw Zig traces. | `E_IMPORT_NOT_FOUND` probe; imported `lib.mc` diagnostic points at `lib.mc`. |
| Expected diagnostic failures no longer print Zig error-return traces | Normal user errors no longer look like compiler ICEs. | Unknown identifier probe prints only the MC diagnostic. |
| Monomorphization has limits and generic body prechecks | Polymorphic recursion and invalid instantiated operators fail loudly instead of hanging or reaching backend emission. | `E_MONOMORPHIZATION_LIMIT`; `38eff033 Validate generic instantiation operators in sema`. |
| Closure typing and closure escape checks are enforced | Closure calls cannot silently use the wrong signature or dangling environment. | `tests/spec/closure_typing.mc`; pushed closure soundness fixes. |
| Linear move checks cover loop conditions and short-circuit RHS | Move-only resources cannot be conditionally consumed in a way that leaks or double-frees. | `tests/spec/move_linear.mc`; `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH` probes. |
| Aggregate `uninit` reads are tracked | Struct/array `var x: T = uninit` reads no longer compile before definite initialization. | `tests/spec/initialization.mc`; `tests/c_emit/bad/use_before_init_aggregate.mc`. |
| Extern/export struct-by-value ABI hazards fail closed | Unsupported C ABI aggregate passing is rejected instead of mislowered by LLVM. | `tests/c_emit/bad/extern_struct_return_by_value.mc`; `tests/c_emit/bad/export_struct_return_by_value.mc`. |
| 128-bit comptime/reflection overflow is guarded | Huge layout/reflection expressions return diagnostics instead of panicking the compiler. | `tests/spec/reflection.mc`; `src/eval_tests.zig` array-size helper tests. |
| `cstr` is implemented and documented | The normative FFI string type now exists across sema, MIR, C, and LLVM lowering. | `1f5c0274 Implement cstr FFI type`; `7278d844 docs: sync cstr FFI status`. |
| Async control-flow spec matches implementation | The spec no longer claims completed E3a/E3b/E3c async forms are reserved. | `b4650dab docs: sync async control-flow spec`; `zig build test`. |
| KASAN/KMSAN store-side sanitizer gaps are closed | Sanitizer modes catch freed/uninitialized heap state on stores as well as loads. | `5b25e328`, `ba8b8de9`. |
| LLVM direct global race lowering is no longer UB-bearing | Direct global scalar, struct-field, and array-element accesses now lower to unordered LLVM atomics instead of plain `load`/`store`. | `9ca762fc Lower racing globals to unordered LLVM atomics`; `llvm-as` on `data_race_semantics` IR. |
| LLVM bounded pointer-mediated global race lowering is no longer UB-bearing | Direct `(&global).*` and local pointer slots initialized from direct global storage, including simple pointer-local copies, lower scalar deref loads/stores to unordered LLVM atomics; broader escaped/computed provenance remains pending. | `cf8b2fdd Lower global pointer derefs to LLVM atomics`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `llvm-as` on `data_race_semantics` IR. |
| LLVM raw-many offset pointer derefs are bounded and conservative | Raw-many pointer locals initialized from already-proven global-backed storage preserve provenance through constant `.offset(0)` and lower the final scalar deref as unordered atomic. Nonzero, dynamic, and unknown call-produced offsets do not claim global provenance, but their scalar derefs now lower conservatively to unordered atomics instead of plain loads. | `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `possibly_racing_raw_many_offset_zero_pointer_load` / `raw_many_offset_one_pointer_lowers_atomic` / `raw_many_offset_dynamic_pointer_lowers_atomic` / `raw_many_offset_unknown_pointer_lowers_atomic`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` raw-many offset assertions; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `pointer_fact_raw_many_nonzero_lowers_race_tolerant` / `pointer_fact_raw_many_dynamic_lowers_race_tolerant` / `pointer_fact_raw_many_unknown_lowers_race_tolerant`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM returned global-pointer race lowering is no longer UB-bearing | Internal helpers proven to return visible global-backed pointer expressions now preserve that provenance at call sites, so scalar derefs of the returned pointer lower to unordered atomics. | `0fb49f96 Lower returned global pointers atomically in LLVM`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `returned_global_pointer`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM scalar pointer-return fallback is retired | LLVM no longer scans function bodies into `global_pointer_return_fns` or treats returned-call expressions as backend-local global proofs. Supported direct, forwarded, noalias-wrapped, branched, and local-function-alias return flows are represented by caller MIR facts; missing or unsupported return facts remain unknown and final scalar dereferences use the atomic default. Aggregate-return summaries remain separate. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of `global_pointer_return_fns` and `collectGlobalPointerProvenanceSummaries`; `src/mir.zig` `collectDirectGlobalPointerReturnSummaries`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM consumes MIR facts for direct internal global pointer returns`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM global pointer-local fallback is retired | C pointer-like local initialization and reassignment are MIR-only. LLVM removes its final `updatePointerGlobalProvenance` ladder: covered direct forms without a MIR fact remain unknown and lower atomically. LLVM retains only a registered local-storage proof for non-MIR aggregate-alias shapes, preserving plain access to storage already proven local without recreating a global proof. Aggregate aliases, field facts, arrays, slices, and aggregate-return summaries remain separate bounded mechanisms. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `updatePointerProvenanceFromMirOrLocalProof` / `updatePointerProvenanceAssignmentFromMirOrLocalProof`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` MIR-only matching helpers; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` and `src/lower_c_tests.zig` missing-pointer-provenance suites; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Direct local aggregate-pointer aliases are MIR-owned | MIR now emits normal destination facts for direct field and constant-index pointer-array reads through a local alias initialized from `&local_aggregate`. Alias writes retain an alias-scoped field fact while invalidating the original aggregate path, so direct and alias reads remain conservative where the existing semantics require it. C and LLVM consume the destination facts; deleting one makes the final scalar access race-tolerant rather than rebuilding an alias proof. | `src/mir.zig` local aggregate alias map and alias-scoped field facts; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records direct local aggregate pointer alias provenance facts`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` local aggregate alias missing-destination suites; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| Direct local fixed-pointer-array aliases are MIR-owned | MIR now emits a normal destination fact for a constant-index read through a local pointer initialized directly from `&ptrs`, such as `pa.*[0]`. A write through the alias invalidates the backing array facts; dynamic alias indexes remain in the separate all-elements fallback boundary. C and LLVM consume the destination fact, and deleting it makes the final scalar access race-tolerant rather than rebuilding LLVM's local pointer-array alias proof. | `src/mir.zig` local pointer-array alias map and invalidation; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records direct local pointer-array alias provenance facts`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` local pointer-array alias missing-destination suites; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| Dynamic all-elements local fixed-pointer-array aliases are MIR-owned | MIR now emits a destination fact for `pa.*[i]` when every backing pointer-array element has the same live `local_storage` or `global_storage` provenance. Mixed, invalidated, and reassigned aliases remain unknown. C and LLVM consume the destination fact; deleting it makes the scalar dereference race-tolerant rather than using LLVM's all-elements alias proof. | `src/mir.zig` `dynamicLocalPointerArrayAliasElementProvenance` / `allLivePointerArrayElementProvenance`; `src/mir_tests.zig` dynamic all-local/all-global/mixed alias cases; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` dynamic local pointer-array alias missing-destination suites; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM scalar pointer parameters fail closed without MIR facts | Scalar pointer parameter call-site summaries, including direct and function-pointer-alias call paths, no longer seed LLVM-local global/local provenance. In the absence of a typed MIR parameter fact, scalar parameter derefs use the established unordered-atomic default, matching the aggregate parameter policy. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of scalar parameter summary collection/seeding; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `consume_global_param` / `consume_local_only_param` / `consume_indirect_local_param`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "ordinary global scalar accesses"`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM direct scalar parameter summaries are retired | A direct internal call that passes `&global` or `&local` no longer grants the callee's scalar pointer parameter a backend-local provenance proof. Both paths lower atomically unless a future typed MIR parameter fact supplies a positive local proof. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of `global_pointer_params` and scalar parameter seeding; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `consume_global_param` / `consume_local_only_param`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "ordinary global scalar accesses"`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM scalar function-pointer parameter inference is retired | Local function-pointer aliases no longer form backend-local scalar parameter provenance proofs. Direct, copied, reassigned, escaped, mixed, and uncalled scalar parameter shapes all remain safe through atomic lowering until a typed MIR parameter-summary family exists. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of scalar parameter call-site collector; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` scalar parameter fixtures; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "ordinary global scalar accesses"`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM function-pointer alias parameter inference is retired | LLVM no longer follows local function-pointer aliases to infer pointer parameter provenance. Without a typed MIR parameter fact, scalar and aggregate pointer parameter dereferences use the conservative atomic path, so they do not depend on LLVM-local call-site inference. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removed parameter alias collectors; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM aggregate-contained pointer field race lowering is no longer UB-bearing for bounded local fields | Direct local aggregate pointer fields initialized or assigned from visible global storage now seed local pointer copies as global-backed during LLVM emission; stack-backed, reassigned stack-backed, whole-aggregate copy, and exported-return ambiguity cases remain plain. | `49f02b3f Track aggregate pointer field provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_global_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_reassigned_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_whole_copy_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_exported_return_pointer_field_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM aggregate whole-copy pointer field provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct same-struct local-to-local aggregate assignment/init copies now propagate already-proven pointer-field facts, so copied global-backed fields continue to lower derefs as unordered atomics while stack-backed and computed aggregate sources remain plain. | `352be47f Propagate aggregate copy pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_whole_copy_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_init_copy_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_whole_copy_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_computed_copy_pointer_field_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM nested aggregate pointer field provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct local named member paths such as `outer.inner.ptr` now carry proven global-backed pointer-field facts through struct-literal init and direct nested field assignment; stack-backed and reassigned-stack nested paths remain plain. | `fd48f50a Track nested aggregate pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `nested_aggregate_global_pointer_field_load` / `nested_aggregate_assigned_global_pointer_field_load` / `nested_aggregate_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `nested_aggregate_reassigned_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM local pointer-array provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct local fixed arrays of pointer-like elements now carry proven global-backed facts for constant-index literal elements and constant-index assignments; stack-backed elements and dynamic-index reads/writes remain plain. | `9f24297e Track LLVM local array pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `array_global_pointer_element_load` / `array_assigned_global_pointer_element_load` / `array_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `array_dynamic_index_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `array_dynamic_assignment_clears_pointer_element_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM local aggregate-pointer aliases are bounded and conservative | Local pointer variables declared directly from `&local_aggregate` now resolve member-path pointer facts through the original aggregate, including nested paths; stack-backed fields, returned/external aggregate pointers, and reassigned unknown aliases remain plain. Aggregate pointer parameters without MIR facts are not local aliases and lower final scalar dereferences atomically. | `f4f13294 Track local aggregate pointer aliases in LLVM`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_pointer_alias_global_pointer_field_load` / `nested_aggregate_pointer_alias_global_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_returned_unknown_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_param_field_lowers_atomic` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_reassigned_unknown_lowers_atomic`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM aggregate array pointer provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct local aggregate fields whose type is a fixed array of pointer-like elements now carry proven global-backed facts for constant-index literal elements and constant-index assignments; stack-backed elements, dynamic-index reads, and dynamic-index writes remain plain. | `5f493f09 Track aggregate array pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_array_global_pointer_element_load` / `aggregate_array_assigned_global_pointer_element_load` / `aggregate_array_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_index_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_assignment_clears_pointer_element_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM all-global dynamic-index pointer array reads are bounded and conservative | Direct local fixed pointer arrays and direct local aggregate pointer-array fields now lower dynamic-index derefs as unordered atomics only when every possible element is proven global-backed; partial arrays and arrays invalidated by dynamic writes remain plain, and the proof fails fast for large/incomplete arrays. | `0e1ae09d Lower dynamic global-backed pointer array reads`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `array_dynamic_index_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `array_dynamic_index_assigned_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `array_dynamic_index_partial_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `array_dynamic_assignment_clears_pointer_element_fact` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_index_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_index_assigned_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_index_partial_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_assignment_clears_pointer_element_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM aggregate pointer aliases compose with pointer-array fields | Local aggregate pointer aliases from direct `&local_aggregate` now resolve fixed pointer-array field element facts through the original aggregate for constant-index reads and all-global dynamic-index reads, while stack-backed, partial dynamic, returned/external, and reassigned aliases remain plain. | `f5223b8e Handle alias aggregate pointer arrays`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_global_pointer_element_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_index_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_index_partial_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_returned_unknown_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_reassigned_unknown_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM aggregate pointer alias writes no longer leave stale provenance | Writes through local aggregate pointer aliases now update or clear the original aggregate's pointer-field and pointer-array facts, including dynamic-index array writes; reassigned/unknown aliases still do not mutate old local facts. Alias field writes to local storage now establish local alias-field facts, so reads back through that alias stay plain. | `b6f7365d Fix aggregate alias pointer write provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_pointer_alias_field_assignment_clears_direct_field_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_field_assignment_establishes_alias_local_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_field_assignment_establishes_global_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_reassigned_unknown_write_does_not_clear_old_field_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_assignment_clears_element_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_assignment_clears_all_element_facts` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_assignment_establishes_element_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_index_assigned_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_index_partially_assigned_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM local slice pointer provenance is bounded and conservative | Local slice variables initialized from direct full-range slices of direct local fixed pointer arrays now preserve all-global pointer provenance for indexed reads; partial, backing-array writes, whole backing-array assignment, slice writes, slice reassignment, and calls clear or avoid the global fact and lower conservatively when no positive local proof exists. | `7637af95 Track LLVM slice pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `slice_global_pointer_element_load` / `slice_assigned_global_pointer_element_load` / `slice_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `slice_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `slice_backing_array_assignment_clears_fact` / `slice_backing_array_dynamic_assignment_clears_fact` / `slice_backing_array_whole_assignment_clears_fact` / `slice_element_assignment_clears_fact` / `slice_reassignment_to_local_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM aggregate pointer-array slice provenance is bounded and conservative | Full-range local slices of direct local aggregate pointer-array fields, including fields reached through local aggregate pointer aliases, now preserve all-global pointer provenance for indexed reads; partial-range, backing aggregate writes, alias writes, and slice writes remain conservative or clear facts when no positive local proof exists. | `77b24fcd Preserve aggregate pointer slice provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_slice_global_pointer_element_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_slice_global_pointer_element_load` / `aggregate_slice_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_slice_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_slice_backing_array_assignment_clears_fact` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_slice_backing_assignment_clears_fact` / `aggregate_slice_element_assignment_clears_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM local pointer-to-array provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct local pointers initialized from `&local_fixed_pointer_array` now preserve all-global pointer provenance for dynamic indexed reads through `pa.*[index]`; stack-backed, partial, reassigned, call-crossing, and backing-write cases remain plain or conservatively clear facts. | `80d7b214 Prove local pointer array aliases in LLVM lowering`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `pointer_to_array_dynamic_index_all_global_pointer_elements_load` / `pointer_to_array_stack_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `pointer_to_array_partial_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `pointer_to_array_reassigned_pointer_stays_plain` / `pointer_to_array_backing_array_write_clears_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`. |
| LLVM partial dynamic pointer-array reads are conservatively atomic | Dynamic-index reads from tracked pointer arrays, pointer-array fields, aggregate pointer aliases, full-range slices, and pointer-to-array aliases now lower the final scalar deref as unordered atomic when any possible backing element is proven global-backed; constant-index reads remain exact, and direct fixed-array / pointer-to-array all-local sets stay plain where positive local facts exist. | `adc3ac8f Conservatively lower partial dynamic pointer arrays`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `array_dynamic_index_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `array_dynamic_index_all_local_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `aggregate_array_dynamic_index_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_index_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_slice_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_slice_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `slice_partial_pointer_elements_load` / `pointer_to_array_partial_pointer_elements_load`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`. |
| LLVM all-local direct pointer-array dynamic reads preserve local provenance | LLVM now keeps `local_storage` as a first-class fixed local pointer-array element fact instead of collapsing non-global elements to unknown. Dynamic reads from direct local fixed pointer arrays, and from direct local pointer-to-array aliases backed by all-local elements, seed the destination pointer local as proven local so the final scalar deref stays plain; partial/global, reassigned, slice-backed, and aggregate-backed dynamic reads remain conservative. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `local_array_global_pointer_elements` stores `mir.PointerProvenance`, `localArrayAllElementsHaveLocalPointerProvenance`, `directLocalArrayBaseHasAllLocalPointerProvenance`, `localPointerArrayAliasBaseHasAllLocalPointerProvenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `array_dynamic_index_all_local_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `pointer_to_array_stack_pointer_elements_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM all-local aggregate pointer-array dynamic reads preserve local provenance | LLVM aggregate pointer-field facts now preserve `local_storage` as well as `global_storage`. Constant and dynamic reads from direct aggregate pointer-array fields, and from local aggregate pointer aliases, keep proven-local elements plain when every possible element is local; partial/global, reassigned, returned, and slice-backed cases remain conservative. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `aggregate_global_pointer_fields` stores `mir.PointerProvenance`, `localAggregateFieldHasLocalPointerProvenance`, `localAggregateArrayAllElementsHaveLocalPointerProvenance`, `directLocalAggregateArrayBaseHasAllLocalPointerProvenance`, `aggregatePointerAliasArrayBaseHasAllLocalPointerProvenance`, and `pointerExprStorageProvenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_array_dynamic_index_all_local_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_array_dynamic_index_all_local_pointer_elements_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM all-local pointer slices preserve local provenance | LLVM now tracks slice ranges whose possible backing pointer elements are all `local_storage`, not only slices with a global-backed element. Constant-index and dynamic-index reads from direct fixed-array slices, direct aggregate pointer-array field slices, and aggregate pointer-alias field slices seed the destination pointer as proven local when the selected or possible backing elements are all local; mixed/global, invalidated backing writes, and unknown slice writes remain conservative. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `directLocalArraySliceBase`, `directLocalAggregateArraySliceBase`, `localSliceElementHasLocalPointerProvenance`, `localSliceAllElementsHaveLocalPointerProvenance`, and `localSliceAnyElementHasGlobalPointerProvenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `slice_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `slice_partial_constant_stack_element_stays_plain` / `slice_partial_range_all_local_stays_plain` / `slice_dynamic_end_all_local_stays_plain` / `slice_dynamic_start_all_local_stays_plain` / `slice_reassignment_to_local_stays_plain` / `aggregate_slice_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_slice_partial_range_all_local_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM constant partial-range pointer slices preserve provenance | Constant, in-bounds partial-range slices of direct local fixed pointer arrays and direct/alias aggregate pointer-array fields now retain backing range metadata; dynamic reads are conservatively atomic when any included backing element is global-backed, constant reads map through the slice offset to exact backing global element provenance, and all-local ranges now preserve local provenance. | `8a412ab1 Track partial pointer slice provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `slice_partial_range_pointer_elements_load` / `slice_partial_range_constant_global_element_load` / `slice_partial_range_constant_stack_element_stays_plain` / `slice_partial_range_all_local_stays_plain` / `aggregate_slice_partial_range_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_slice_partial_range_pointer_elements_load` / `aggregate_slice_partial_range_constant_global_element_load` / `aggregate_slice_partial_range_constant_stack_element_stays_plain` / `aggregate_slice_partial_range_all_local_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`. |
| LLVM aggregate pointer parameters fail closed without MIR facts | LLVM no longer summarizes direct-call aggregate pointer fields in the callee. | C noalias pointer-container classifier is fail-closed on malformed calls | The C typed-provenance direct-address classifier now requires the real `compiler.assume_noalias_unchecked` builtin shape before reading the wrapped pointer expression: no type arguments and exactly two call arguments. That matches the MIR/LLVM guarded classifiers and keeps malformed or partially recovered noalias call shapes from participating in direct pointer-container fact ownership. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `directMirAddressProvenanceExpr`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "without MIR destination"`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR and LLVM noalias pointer-container classifiers require the real builtin signature | MIR pointer-provenance production and LLVM's typed-MIR direct-address classifier now agree that `compiler.assume_noalias_unchecked` is MIR-owned only for the real builtin shape: no type arguments and exactly two call arguments. Malformed or partially recovered same-named calls no longer participate in direct pointer-container fact production or covered LLVM MIR-consumption cleanup. | `src/mir.zig` `directAddressProvenance`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `directMirAddressProvenanceExpr`; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer provenance"`; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "without MIR"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM noalias fallback provenance classifiers are fail-closed on malformed calls | LLVM's remaining backend-local noalias wrappers require the real builtin shape before using the wrapped pointer expression for direct fallback provenance or expression typing. Malformed or partially recovered same-named calls cannot seed fallback global/local provenance outside the stricter MIR-owned classifier. Scalar parameter and scalar return summaries are retired separately. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `directMirAddressProvenanceExpr`, `pointerExprHasGlobalStorageProvenance`, and `exprType`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM direct pointer locals without MIR facts lower conservatively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "without MIR"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM raw-many offset fallback classifier is fail-closed on malformed calls | LLVM's shared raw-many `.offset` classifier now rejects malformed same-named calls before type/provenance queries can use the base expression: no type arguments and exactly one offset argument are required. This keeps raw-many fallback typing and provenance aligned with the stricter MIR-owned raw-many zero-offset classifier. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `rawManyOffsetCallInfo`, `pointerExprHasGlobalStorageProvenance`, `emitBuiltinValueCall`, and `exprType`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM raw-many zero direct local without MIR fact lowers conservatively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "without MIR"`; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR pointer provenance covers const-global zero/index direct pointer containers | The typed MIR pointer-provenance producer now uses the builder's compile-time `usize` evaluator for direct raw-many `.offset(0)`, fixed pointer-array element reads, aggregate pointer-array element reads, and aggregate pointer-array element assignments. Const-global forms such as `p.offset(ZERO)` and `ptrs[FIRST_INDEX]` now emit the same `PointerProvenanceFact` rows as literal zero/index forms, and C/LLVM consume those facts instead of relying on backend-local constant-index recognition. | `src/mir.zig` `rawManyZeroOffsetProvenance`, `constantIndexLocalPointerElementProvenance`, `directAggregatePointerArrayElementProvenance`, `directLocalAggregateArrayElementPath`, and aggregate index assignment provenance; `src/mir_tests.zig` const-global raw-many and pointer-array provenance fixtures; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `pointer_fact_raw_many_zero_const_global_load`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `raw_many_zero_const_global_requires_mir_fact`; focused raw-many/fixed-array MIR/C/LLVM tests; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR pointer provenance covers reflection-derived zero/index direct pointer containers | MIR's pointer-provenance compile-time index evaluator now handles const globals whose values come from reflection folding, so shapes such as `p.offset(REFLECT_ZERO_OFFSET)` and `ptrs[REFLECT_INDEX]` where the constants are `field_offset<ZeroField>(.value)` produce authoritative `PointerProvenanceFact` rows. C and LLVM consume the reflected raw-many zero fact, and LLVM's missing-destination-fact test proves reflected fixed pointer-array reads still require the MIR destination fact. | `src/mir.zig` `constUsizeValue` with `parseArrayLenWithReflect`; `src/mir_tests.zig` reflected raw-many/fixed-array/aggregate pointer-array provenance fixtures; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `pointer_fact_raw_many_zero_reflect_load`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `raw_many_zero_reflect_requires_mir_fact` / `pointer_array_element_reflect_read_requires_mir_fact`; focused MIR/C/LLVM pointer-provenance tests; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR reflection calls preserve live pointer provenance | Direct compile-time reflection calls used inside pointer-container expressions, such as `p.offset(field_offset<ZeroField>(.value))` and `ptrs[field_offset<ZeroField>(.value)]`, no longer look like ordinary mutating calls to the MIR pointer-provenance tracker. Well-shaped reflection calls are now treated as provenance-preserving, so direct reflected zero/index expressions keep live array/raw-many facts and emit destination `PointerProvenanceFact` rows; malformed reflection-like calls still use the old invalidating path. | `src/mir.zig` `reflectionCallPreservesPointerProvenance`; `src/mir_tests.zig` direct reflected raw-many/fixed-array/aggregate pointer-array provenance fixtures; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `pointer_fact_raw_many_zero_reflect_load`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `raw_many_zero_reflect_requires_mir_fact` / `pointer_array_element_reflect_read_requires_mir_fact`; focused MIR/C/LLVM pointer-provenance tests; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM same-struct aggregate copies no longer carry dead backend-local provenance fallback | The direct local same-struct aggregate copy route now relies on MIR aggregate `field_path` facts before any aggregate field cache is populated. The old `tryCopyAggregatePointerFieldProvenanceFromLocal` backend-local cache-copy helper was unreachable for direct local aggregate copies and has been removed, keeping Phase 5 cleanup honest: missing field facts leave covered direct aggregate derefs conservative instead of preserving a stale backend-only proof. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `updateAggregatePointerFieldProvenanceFromInit`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` aggregate pointer-field and pointer-array missing-fact fixtures; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "aggregate pointer-field reads without MIR destination fact"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "aggregate pointer-array element reads without MIR destination fact"`; `git diff --check`. |
| C fixed pointer-array destination provenance no longer has a backend-local fallback | The direct fixed pointer-array element read path is now fully MIR-owned for pointer-like local initializers and assignments. If the destination MIR `PointerProvenanceFact` is missing, C leaves the destination provenance unknown instead of reconstructing global storage from the local array-element cache through a backend-local fallback. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `directMirFixedPointerArrayElementExpr`, `updatePointerProvenanceFromMir`, and `updatePointerProvenanceAssignmentFromMir`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "fixed pointer-array element reads without MIR destination fact"`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "without MIR"`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| C aggregate pointer-read provenance fails closed without destination MIR facts | C now has explicit negative coverage matching the LLVM missing-fact tests for direct aggregate pointer-field and aggregate pointer-array element destination reads, including assignment, same-struct copy, and nested aggregate paths. Removing the destination `PointerProvenanceFact` for `p` suppresses the consumed-fact comment and keeps the scalar deref on the conservative race-tolerant path instead of recreating backend-local global provenance. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `appendCheckedCTestWithoutPointerProvenanceFactsForSubject`, `clearPointerProvenanceFactsForFunctionSubject`, and `lower-c aggregate pointer reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "aggregate pointer reads without MIR destination fact"`; `git diff --check`. |

C and LLVM consume those field-path facts for direct aggregate derefs, and tests with the aggregate field fact removed keep the deref on the conservative race-tolerant path without a consumed field-provenance comment. | `src/mir.zig` `directPointerProvenance` use in aggregate pointer-field producers; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records aggregate pointer assignments from pointer-local copy facts`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `c_aggregate_field_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `c_aggregate_array_element_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `aggregate_field_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `aggregate_array_element_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact`; focused C/LLVM aggregate missing-field tests; `git diff --check`. |
| Typed semantic facts cover aggregate raw-many zero pointer updates | MIR now records aggregate pointer-field and aggregate pointer-array element provenance when direct aggregate assignments use live raw-many `.offset(0)` expressions. | LLVM aggregate-return summary collectors use MIR direct-local provenance where covered | LLVM aggregate-return summary collection seeds direct pointer-like local provenance from matching MIR `PointerProvenanceFact` source points for the same bounded direct-local/direct-copy/raw-many-zero shapes used by emission, instead of re-running `updatePointerGlobalProvenance` for those covered forms. | Consistent internal global pointer branch returns are MIR-owned | MIR now joins direct `return &global` exits across an internal helper's terminating `if`/switch arms, including helpers with ordinary value parameters. It emits a caller `PointerProvenanceFact` only when every modeled exit agrees on the same global; mixed return storage or possible fallthrough remains unknown and therefore lowers race-tolerantly. C and LLVM consume the caller fact at the call-result local, while removing it still preserves the conservative path. Exported, callback, loop, and arbitrary return-flow summaries remain pending. | `src/mir.zig` `collectDirectGlobalPointerReturnSummaries`, `directGlobalReturnFlowForBlock`, and `directPointerProvenance`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR joins consistent internal global pointer returns across branches`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` direct-return fact tests; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR tracks straight-line local function aliases for proven pointer returns | A local function-pointer alias initialized directly from an internal helper with an existing global-pointer return summary can now seed the call-result `PointerProvenanceFact`. The alias target is dropped on reassignment, indirect store, address escape, and branch/switch/loop control-flow boundaries, so callbacks, escaped aliases, and joined aliases remain unknown and lower race-tolerantly. C and LLVM consume the resulting ordinary caller fact through their existing missing-fact-gated paths. | `src/mir.zig` `local_function_aliases`, `directPointerReturnAliasTarget`, and alias invalidation; `src/mir_tests.zig` local function-alias return provenance; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` direct-return fact tests; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| Bounds checks require typed MIR facts | Non-elided array-index and slice bounds checks now record owned `BoundsFact` entries in MIR. This is a bounded bounds-fact family slice, not closure of every range/defaulting decision. | `src/mir_model.zig` `BoundsFact`; `src/mir.zig` index/slice producers; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` / `src/lower_llvm.zig` `requireMirBoundsFact`; C/LLVM missing-fact tests; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |

| Typed semantic facts inventory pins no-overflow range consumers | The semantic-facts inventory now exact-counts the C `hasMirNoOverflowRangeFact` arith hook, the LLVM `requireMirNoOverflowRangeFact` gate, the LLVM range-target context, and the LLVM consumed-fact comment. New unchecked-arithmetic backend paths now fail the inventory gate unless they keep routing through the typed MIR no-overflow range consumer or deliberately update the register. | `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py` `ANCHORS` / `EXACT_COUNTS`; `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md` MIR no-overflow range facts row; `src/mir_model.zig` `RangeFact`; `src/mir.zig` `mir range_fact`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `hasMirNoOverflowRangeFact`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `requireMirNoOverflowRangeFact`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM unchecked arithmetic consumes MIR no-overflow range facts | LLVM no longer lowers `unchecked.add/sub/mul` solely because the AST call is inside the accepted unsafe-contract syntax. The unchecked builtin path now requires a matching MIR `RangeFact` at the call source point, emits a `; mir range_fact consumed ... assumption=no_overflow` comment when it uses the fact, and fails closed if a prebuilt MIR module lacks that fact. This is a bounded typed-fact-family slice, not full closure of typed MIR. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `requireMirNoOverflowRangeFact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact`; `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md` range-fact consumer row; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM no-overflow range facts require target identity | LLVM now matches MIR `RangeFact` rows by target label as well as operation and source point before lowering `unchecked.add/sub/mul` as plain arithmetic. Return values, local initializers, assignments, call arguments, binary operands, and aggregate literal leaves set the expected target while emitting, and a prebuilt MIR module whose otherwise matching range fact is retargeted now fails closed. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `current_mir_range_target`, `emitExprWithMirRangeTarget`, and `requireMirNoOverflowRangeFact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `appendLlvmTestWithRetargetedRangeFacts`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM no-overflow range fact target coverage matches MIR producers | LLVM regression coverage now exercises the MIR range-fact target labels emitted for return values, inferred locals, assignments, call arguments, binary operands, array literal elements, and struct literal fields. | MIR representation facts are explicit in lower-mir dumps | Representation-sensitive typed loads, checks, and uses now emit stable `mir representation_fact ... recorded=true` rows with type and `value_id`, alongside ordinary instruction rows. | MIR representation facts are first-class typed MIR rows | Representation-sensitive typed loads, checks, and uses are now recorded in `Function.representation_facts` as owned `RepresentationFact` entries keyed by kind, type, `value_id`, and source point. The lower-mir and MIR verification artifacts print those owned rows instead of rediscovering them from instruction kinds, and tests assert both the in-memory fact slice and dump text. | `src/mir_model.zig` `RepresentationFact`; `src/mir.zig` `representation_facts`, `representationFactKind`, `appendDumpOpt`, and `appendVerificationFacts`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR dump exposes representation value identities`; `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md`; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C and LLVM consume representation facts as a MIR admission gate | Both production backends now reject prebuilt MIR when an owned `RepresentationFact` is missing or no longer exactly matches its representation-sensitive instruction. This makes the fact slice load-bearing at backend entry and prevents a mutated MIR artifact from falling through to AST-only representation trust. | `src/mir.zig` `validateRepresentationFactsForLowering`; `src/lower_c.zig` `appendCProfileWithMir`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `appendLlvmCheckedMir`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` missing and stale representation-fact tests; focused C/LLVM tests; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| Integer literal syntax overflow rejects before defaulting | Oversized integer literal syntax is treated as an out-of-range semantic error instead of falling through to target defaulting or backend emission. The semantic-facts inventory anchors the shared `parseIntegerLiteral` overflow sentinel, the initializer/targetless/binary-operand semantic gates, and exact fixture counts across binary operands, annotated locals, targetless locals, globals, and returns. This is a bounded integer/defaulting cleanup slice, not closure of every integer/default fact family. | `src/numeric.zig` `parseIntegerLiteral`; `src/sema.zig` `integerLiteralSyntaxOverflow`, `checkIntegerLiteralInitializer`, `checkTargetlessLiteralInitializer`, and `checkLiteralOperandAgainstClass`; `tests/spec/no_implicit_conversion.mc`; `tests/spec/initialization.mc`; `tests/spec/global_initializers.mc`; `tests/spec/return_types.mc`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig --test-filter "tests/spec fixtures produce declared semantic error codes"`; `git diff --check`. |
| Lexer skips UTF-8 BOM at file start | Source files that begin with a UTF-8 byte-order mark now lex as ordinary MC files instead of reporting `E_LEX_UNEXPECTED_BYTE`. The lexer advances past the BOM while preserving the first real token at line 1, column 1, and the unit test locks that diagnostic-free behavior. | `src/lexer.zig` `Lexer.init`; `src/lexer_tests.zig` `lexer skips UTF-8 BOM at start of file`; `zig test src/lexer_tests.zig --test-filter "UTF-8 BOM"`; `python3 tools/toolchain/readiness-ledger-test.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR aggregate representation facts expose stable value identities | Aggregate field and array-element representation uses now have explicit lower-MIR dump coverage, not only verifier rows. Casted pointer values stored into struct fields or array elements emit owned `mir representation_fact ... detail=aggregate_field/aggregate_element ... value_id=cast` rows, proving aggregate representation obligations are auditable through the typed MIR artifact. | `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR target representation checks see through casts`; `src/mir.zig` `addRepresentationUseForValue` / `appendDumpOpt`; `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md`; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig --test-filter "MIR target representation checks see through casts"`; `git diff --check`. |
| Semantic fact inventory guards representation fact rows | The Phase 1 inventory checker now anchors the `lower-mir` representation fact surface, including instruction `value_id` text and explicit `mir representation_fact` rows, so future edits cannot silently drop the artifact coverage added for representation-sensitive typed loads/checks/uses. | `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `src/mir.zig` `appendDumpOpt`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR dump exposes representation value identities`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| C unchecked arithmetic consumes MIR no-overflow range facts | C lowering no longer has a generic unchecked-arithmetic builtin fallback that can emit plain C arithmetic solely from AST syntax. The existing specialized unchecked paths still emit only when a matching MIR `RangeFact` is present, and a prebuilt MIR module with that fact removed now fails closed with `UnsupportedCEmission`. This is a bounded typed-fact-family cleanup, not full closure of typed MIR. | `src/lower_c_builtin_emit.zig` `uncheckedNoOverflowCallOp`; `src/lower_c_arith.zig` `emitUncheckedAddValueTempFromCall`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `hasMirNoOverflowRangeFact`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact`; `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md` range-fact consumer row; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C no-overflow range facts fail closed on target mismatch | C now has an explicit prebuilt-MIR negative test matching the LLVM retargeted-fact regression: changing an otherwise matching `RangeFact.target` suppresses unchecked arithmetic lowering and returns `UnsupportedCEmission`. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `retargetRangeFactsForFunction`, `appendCheckedCTestWithRetargetedRangeFacts`, and `lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact"`. |
| C no-overflow range fact target coverage matches MIR producers | C regression coverage now exercises the MIR range-fact target labels emitted for return values, inferred locals, assignments, call arguments, binary operands, array literal elements, and struct literal fields, and retargets a struct-field fact to prove non-`value` targets fail closed too. This aligns the C typed-fact gate with the existing LLVM target-identity evidence. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact`; expected `MC_MIR_RANGE` comments for `target=value`, `target=inferred`, `target=sum`, `target=call_arg`, `target=binary_operand`, `target=aggregate_element`, and `target=next`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact"`. |
| C direct raw-many offset derefs lower race-tolerantly | The C backend now covers the sequenced raw-many `.offset(...).*` access class for scalar pointees. Direct local-base offsets can lower inline through `mc_race_load_*`, and call-produced bases are sequenced into pointer temps before a race-tolerant load temp, avoiding the previous plain `*mc_tmp` load for that access class. This is a bounded slice of broader pointer-provenance race lowering, not full closure. | `src/lower_c_access.zig` `emitRawManyOffsetDerefValueTemp`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceLoadTempFromPointerTemp`; `src/lower_c_infer.zig` `derefPointeeType`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `direct_raw_many_offset_lowers_race_tolerant` / `direct_call_raw_many_offset_lowers_race_tolerant`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C pointer-member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly | Ordinary scalar field loads/stores through pointer bases, including call-produced aggregate pointers, no longer emit plain `p->field` / `p->field = value` when locality is not proven. Scalar fields route through `mc_race_load_*` / `mc_race_store_*`, pointer-shaped fields use relaxed C atomics, and direct aggregate fields are handled by the recursive aggregate slice below. This is a bounded aggregate access-class slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberLoadExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberStoreStmt`, `exprHasPointerType`, and `memberFieldType`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c pointer member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C nested pointer-member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly | Nested scalar fields reached through pointer bases, such as `p.inner.value` and `external_outer().inner.value`, now build the full field address and use race helpers or relaxed atomics instead of plain C nested field loads/stores. Aggregate-width pointer-member value copies still fail closed. This is a bounded nested aggregate access-class slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `collectPointerMemberPath`, `emitPointerMemberPathAddressExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberLoadExpr`, and `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberStoreStmt`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c nested pointer member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C pointer-member aggregate value copies lower recursively | Direct and nested aggregate field value copies through ambiguous pointer bases no longer fall through to plain `p->field` aggregate reads/writes and no longer fail closed when every leaf has sound scalar/pointer race-tolerant lowering. C now sequences the pointer root, reconstructs aggregate loads from leaf `mc_race_load_*` / relaxed atomic pointer loads, and splits aggregate stores into leaf stores. Proven-local pointer bases still use the existing plain path; unsupported union-like leaves still fail closed. This is a bounded pointer-member aggregate slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberAggregateExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberAggregateExpr`, aggregate branches in `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberStoreStmt` / `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberStoreStmt`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateLoadFromPtr`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateStoreFromPtr`, and `derefPointerHasProvenLocalStorage`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c pointer member aggregate value copies lower field-wise race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer member aggregate"`; `git diff --check`. |

| C aggregate pointer deref value copies lower recursively | Aggregate pointee value copies through unproven pointer derefs no longer fall through to plain `*p` aggregate reads or `*p = value` aggregate writes, and no longer fail closed for struct/fixed-array aggregates whose leaves have sound race-tolerant lowering. | C/LLVM local raw-many zero fixed-array aggregate derefs stay plain | Raw-many zero-offset aliases of fixed-array aggregate structs now have explicit local-storage evidence. | Proven-local fixed-array aggregate pointer deref copies stay plain | C and LLVM now have explicit local-storage evidence for fixed-array aggregate pointer deref value copies. When a `*mut WithArray` is proven to point at local storage, stores through `p.*` and later aggregate copies from `p.*` stay on the plain aggregate path instead of being split into race-tolerant leaf operations. This is a locality evidence slice for the fixed-array aggregate path, not full alias-flow completion. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c fixed-array aggregate pointer deref value copies lower recursively`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM proven-local aggregate pointer deref value copy stays plain`; focused `zig test` filters for those tests; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR representation facts expose cast value identities across use sites | The lower-MIR artifact now has explicit coverage that cast pointer values keep the stable `value_id=cast` identity across return checks, local initializers, assignments, call arguments, aggregate fields, and aggregate elements. This strengthens the typed representation-fact artifact beyond aggregate-only rows; production backend decisions still do not consume this representation fact family. | `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR target representation checks see through casts`; `src/mir.zig` `addInstrWithValue` / `addRepresentationUseForValue` / `appendDumpOpt`; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig --test-filter "MIR target representation checks see through casts"`; `git diff --check`. |
| C consumes MIR no-overflow facts for nested unchecked operands | C lowering now materializes nested `unchecked.add` / `unchecked.sub` / `unchecked.mul` operands inside an enclosing MIR-proven no-overflow expression instead of sending them through the generic builtin-call path. This keeps nested unsafe-contract arithmetic lowering to plain C arithmetic once the enclosing MIR range fact is matched. | `src/lower_c_arith.zig` `emitUncheckedOperandTemp` / `emitUncheckedOperandCallTemp`; `tests/c_emit/mir_value_range_contract.mc` nested-chain fixture; `zig-out/bin/mcc emit-c tests/c_emit/mir_value_range_contract.mc`; `zig build c-test`. |
| LLVM pointer-member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly | Scalar member loads and stores reached through ambiguous pointer bases, including nested member chains and call-produced aggregate pointers, now use unordered atomic LLVM access unless the root pointer is positively proven local. Proven-local pointer-member accesses remain plain. This is a bounded pointer-member scalar slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `scalarPointerMemberBaseUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `pointerMemberRoot`, `emitMemberLoad`, and `emitMemberAssignment`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM pointer-member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer-member scalar"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM pointer-member aggregate value copies lower recursively | Aggregate member value loads/stores reached through ambiguous pointer bases now reuse the recursive aggregate race-tolerant lowering path, reconstructing loads from unordered atomic leaf accesses and splitting stores into unordered atomic leaf stores. This is a bounded pointer-member aggregate slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` aggregate branches in `emitMemberLoad` / `emitMemberAssignment` plus `pointerMemberBaseUsesRaceTolerantLowering`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM pointer-member aggregate value copies lower recursively`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer-member aggregate"`; `git diff --check`. |

| Semantic fact inventory rejects LLVM global fallback provenance | The Phase 1 semantic-facts inventory now requires zero `updatePointerGlobalProvenance` definitions and calls. | Move checker branch joins preserve moved field places | Branch cleanup no longer drops synthetic moved-subplace keys such as `p.a` when the root `p` belongs to the outer state. A field moved out in one branch and left live in another now reaches the branch join and reports `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH`, instead of merging as if only the root binding mattered. This is a bounded CFG/place slice, not the full checker rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `finalizeBranchLocals`, `mergeMoveBranches`, `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`, and `isMoveSubplaceKey`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_branch_partial_field_move`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig build test`. |
| Move checker branch joins preserve wildcard array subplaces | Branch joins now have explicit coverage for wildcard dynamic array-element moves and wildcard dynamic move-struct array-field element moves. Moving `arr[i]` or `box.items[i]` in only one branch reports `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH`, proving dynamic wildcard subplaces are carried to the ordinary branch join instead of being dropped as branch-local state. This is a branch CFG/place evidence slice, not the full checker rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `finalizeBranchLocals`, `mergeMoveBranches`, `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`, and `isMoveSubplaceKey`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_branch_dynamic_array_element_move` / `reject_branch_dynamic_array_field_element_move`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Move checker switch joins preserve moved place state | Switch arm joins now have explicit coverage for the same moved-place state as branch joins. A field, concrete array element, array-field element, wildcard dynamic array element, or wildcard dynamic array-field element moved in one reachable arm and left live in another reports `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH` at the switch join instead of letting the root aggregate continue as whole. | `src/sema_move.zig` switch arm cloning/finalization plus `mergeMoveBranches`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_switch_partial_field_move` / `reject_switch_array_element_move` / `reject_switch_array_field_element_move` / `reject_switch_dynamic_array_element_move` / `reject_switch_dynamic_array_field_element_move`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Move checker short-circuit RHS preserves moved field places | Short-circuit RHS analysis now notices field-place state created only on the conditional RHS, such as `flag && consume(p.a)`, and reports `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH` instead of letting the root binding continue as if the field were consistently owned. This extends the CFG/place join behavior to expression-level branch edges. | `src/sema_move.zig` `moveConsumeShortCircuitRhs`, `isMoveSubplaceKey`, and `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_short_circuit_partial_field_move`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig build test`. |
| Move checker short-circuit RHS preserves concrete array subplaces | Short-circuit RHS analysis now has explicit coverage for concrete fixed-array element moves. `flag && consume(arr[0])` reports `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH` and leaves later whole-array cleanup poisoned, proving stable indexed subplaces are treated like field subplaces on expression-level branch edges. This is a short-circuit CFG/place evidence slice, not the full checker rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `moveConsumeShortCircuitRhs`, `isMoveSubplaceKey`, and `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_short_circuit_array_element_move`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Move checker loops preserve moved field places | Loop analysis now detects moved field-place state created by a `while` condition or loop body, such as `consume(p.a)`, and reports `E_MOVE_LOOP_RESOURCE` because the loop may run zero or multiple times. This extends outer-resource loop checks from whole bindings to nested field places. | `src/sema_move.zig` `reportLoopOuterResourceChanges`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_loop_partial_field_move` / `reject_while_condition_partial_field_move`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig build test`. |
| Move checker scoped blocks preserve moved field places | Lexical block cleanup now restores outer bindings while carrying forward moved subplace records rooted in those outer bindings. A field moved inside `{ ... }` remains poisoned after the block exits, so a later duplicate field move or whole-aggregate move is rejected. This is another bounded CFG/place slice, not the full checker rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `moveScopedBlock` and `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_block_partial_field_move` / `reject_block_whole_after_partial`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig build test`. |
| Move checker scoped blocks preserve field reinitialization | Lexical block cleanup no longer restores a stale moved-subplace marker when the same outer field is reinitialized inside the block. A field moved and then assigned a fresh `move` resource inside `{ ... }` remains usable after the block exits. This is a bounded scoped-place repair, not the full CFG/place rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `moveScopedBlock`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `accept_block_reinitialize_moved_field`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig build test`. |
| Move checker tracks constant-index local array element places | Local fixed arrays that contain linear `move` resources are no longer rejected wholesale. Constant-index element places such as `arr[0]` now behave like field places for duplicate moves, borrow-after-move, reinitialization, branch joins, loop joins, scoped cleanup, and whole-array partial-move checks. This is a bounded indexed-place slice, not the full CFG rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `placeKeyAndType`, `moveIndexedPlaceKey`, `arrayIndexEmbedsMove`, `isMoveSubplaceKey`, `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`, and `reportLoopOuterResourceChanges`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `accept_move_each_array_element` / `accept_reinitialize_array_element` / `reject_duplicate_array_element_move` / `reject_borrow_after_array_element_move` / `reject_branch_array_element_move` / `reject_loop_array_element_move`; `tests/spec/move_container.mc` `accept_move_array_elements`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`. |
| Move checker tracks constant-index array elements inside move-struct fields | `move struct` fields may now own fixed arrays of linear `move` resources by value when elements are accessed through constant-index places such as `box.items[0]`. Those field-element places reuse the existing nested place model for duplicate moves, borrow-after-move, reinitialization, branch joins, and whole-container partial-move checks. Copyable/non-`move` struct fields, globals, extern/export ABI params/returns, and general dynamic indexes remain fail-closed. This is a bounded aggregate/indexed-place slice, not the full CFG/place rewrite. | `src/sema.zig` `checkStruct`; `src/sema_move.zig` `placeKeyAndType`, `moveIndexedPlaceKey`, `placeExprIsMoved`, and `hasMovedSubplace`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `accept_move_array_field_elements` / `accept_reinitialize_array_field_element` / `reject_duplicate_array_field_element_move` / `reject_borrow_after_array_field_element_move` / `reject_whole_after_array_field_partial` / `reject_branch_array_field_element_move`; `tests/spec/bad/move_cfg_arrays_reject.mc`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `python3 tools/toolchain/bad-diagnostics-test.py --check`. |
| Move checker return exits preserve array-element subplaces | Function return leak checks now have explicit coverage for local fixed-array element moves, wildcard dynamic array-element moves, move-struct array field element moves, and wildcard dynamic move-struct array field element moves. These exit edges report `E_RESOURCE_LEAK` instead of treating the partially moved aggregate as fully consumed. | Move checker tracks laundered subplace pointer aliases precisely for stale reads | Pointer-returning direct calls that receive `&pair.a` or `&arr[0]` now register the returned pointer local as an alias of that exact tracked subplace instead of only the root owner. Using the returned pointer after the subplace is moved reports `E_USE_AFTER_MOVE`, while using the pointer before the move remains accepted. The returned pointer still does not gain trusted pointee ownership for arbitrary moves. This is a bounded laundered-subplace stale-alias slice, not full pointer-pointee ownership modeling. | `src/sema_move.zig` `callLaunderedMoveReferent`, `fullDerefMoveSubplaceAlias`, and `checkStaleAlias`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `accept_laundered_subplace_pointer_used_before_move` / `reject_laundered_field_alias_after_move` / `reject_laundered_array_element_alias_after_move`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |

| Move checker re-derives reassigned laundered subplace aliases | Reassigning an existing pointer alias from a pointer-returning direct call, such as `pa = id_res(&pair.a)` or `p0 = id_res(&arr[0])`, now updates the alias referent to the exact tracked subplace. | Move checker tracks deferred borrow liveness | Deferred expressions that borrow move roots or subplaces now reserve that borrow separately from deferred consuming cleanup. | Typed semantic facts cover nested aggregate member struct-literal reassignment pointer fields | MIR now records `PointerProvenanceFact.field_path` rows when assigning a struct literal to a nested aggregate member such as `outer.inner = .{ .ptr = gp, .ptrs = .{ gp, &local } }`. | Typed semantic facts cover nested aggregate literal local pointer-copy fields | Nested aggregate member struct-literal initialization now has explicit local-storage backend evidence for scalar pointer fields. `let outer: Outer = .{ .inner = .{ .ptr = lp } }` keeps `outer.inner.ptr.*` plain on C and LLVM only while the MIR `outer field=inner.ptr` fact is present; deleting that field fact makes both backends lower the deref race-tolerantly instead of recovering local storage from backend-local AST inference. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `c_nested_aggregate_field_literal_local_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `nested_aggregate_field_literal_local_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact`; focused C/LLVM aggregate pointer-field missing-fact tests; `git diff --check`. |

| Typed semantic facts cover nested same-struct aggregate copy pointer fields | Direct same-struct aggregate copy propagation now has explicit nested-field and nested pointer-array element evidence. MIR copies live `field_path` rows such as `inner.ptr` and `inner.ptrs[0]` from `outer` to `copied_outer`; C and LLVM consume those copied nested field facts for direct scalar derefs, while deleting the copied nested field or pointer-array element fact falls back to race-tolerant lowering without preserving a backend-only proof. | `src/mir_tests.zig` `from_copied_nested_field` / `from_copied_nested_field_element`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `c_nested_aggregate_field_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `c_nested_aggregate_array_element_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `copied` `inner.ptr` / `inner.ptrs` fact fixtures; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `nested_aggregate_field_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `nested_aggregate_array_element_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `copied` `inner.ptr` / `inner.ptrs` fact fixtures; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig --test-filter "MIR records typed pointer provenance facts for direct globals and pointer arrays"`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "lower-c aggregate pointer reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-field reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-array element reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`. |

| Lower-MIR artifact exposes nested aggregate copy field-path rows | The `lower-mir` dump now has explicit regression coverage for nested scalar `field_path` rows copied through same-struct aggregate initializer and assignment copies, not only the corresponding pointer-array element rows. | LLVM aggregate struct-literal pointer-copy fields require MIR field facts | LLVM no longer recreates local/global aggregate field provenance from backend-local pointer-copy inference when a direct struct-literal field value is already a MIR-owned pointer container expression but the matching `PointerProvenanceFact.field_path` row is missing. Direct pointer-copy, raw-many zero, noalias/direct address, pointer-array element, and aggregate pointer-field literal values now fail closed to unknown for direct aggregate field caches unless MIR supplies the field fact; the new local pointer-copy negative test proves a missing local `holder.ptr` fact falls back to unordered atomic lowering instead of preserving a backend-only local proof. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `updateAggregatePointerFieldProvenanceFromStructLiteral`, `updateAggregateArrayPointerElementProvenanceFromLiteral`, `updateAggregatePointerFieldProvenanceFromAssignment`, and `directMirPointerContainerValueExpr`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `aggregate_field_local_pointer_copy_literal_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `holder.ptr` fact fixture; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-field reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM aggregate struct-literal pointer-array pointer-copy elements require MIR field facts | The same MIR-owned-pointer-container rule now covers fixed pointer-array elements inside direct struct-literal aggregate fields. A local pointer copied into `.ptrs[0]` keeps plain lowering only when the MIR `holder field=ptrs element=0` fact exists; removing that field fact leaves the aggregate element provenance unknown and lowers the later deref through unordered atomic fallback. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `updateAggregateArrayPointerElementProvenanceFromLiteral` and `directMirPointerContainerValueExpr`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `aggregate_array_element_local_pointer_copy_literal_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `holder.ptrs[0]` fact fixture; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-array element reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `git diff --check`. |

| Move checker treats constant-zero dynamic indexes as concrete places | Runtime-looking index expressions that have only one possible value now fold into the concrete array element place when tracking move resources. `i % 1`, `(i + i) % 2`, `i * 0`, `i - i`, `i & 0`, and `i ^ i` target `arr[0]`; equivalent canonical symbolic forms such as `(i + 1) - j` and `(i + 1) ^ j` also fold to `arr[0]` when `j` carries the same symbolic index.
